<ol><li>rebel</li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:бунтовать.html>бунтова́ть</a> (14379)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бунт.html>бунт</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bunt</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ова́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бунтовать.html>бунтова́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">buntovátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">взбунтова́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">imperfective only</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to revolt, to rebel</li>
<li>to incite a revolt</li></ol>

***бур.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:бурый.html>бур</a> (15356)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Afrikaans" class="extiw" title="w:Afrikaans">Afrikaans</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="af">boer</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">farmer</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бурый.html>бур</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bur</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бурый.html>бу́ра</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бурый.html>бу́ры</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бур.html>бу́ров</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Boer <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">white South African person of Dutch, or by extension other Non-Anglo-Saxon, descent</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms_2">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">бу́рский</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">búrskij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from a Germanic language, probably <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">boor</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">drill</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бурый.html>бур</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bur</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бурый.html>бу́ра</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бурый.html>бу́ры</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бур.html>бу́ров</a></b>, <i>related adjective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:буровой.html>бурово́й</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>bore, drill, auger</li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Persian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Persian language">Persian</a></span> <i class="fa-Arab mention" lang="fa">بوره‎</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="fa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bure</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">borax</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бурый.html>бура́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">burá</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бурый.html>буры́</a></b>, <i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>borax
<ul><li><div class="wiktQuote" data-validation="white">Александр Солженицын, <i>Матренин <a href = vnd.unilang:двор.html>двор</a></i> 1968:<dl><dd><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приносить.html>приноси́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:химический.html>хими́ческого</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:кабинет.html>кабине́та</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:бурый.html>буры́</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:смешивать.html>сме́шивая</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тесто.html>те́стом</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>мы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:таракан.html>тарака́нов</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:травить.html>трави́ли</a></span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">prinosíl ja iz ximíčeskovo kabinéta <b>burý</b>, i, sméšivaja s téstom, my tarakánov travíli</i></dd><dd>From the chemical lab I brought <b>borax</b> and, mixing it with paste, we hunted the cockroaches</dd></dl></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:бурда.html>бурда́</a> (23627)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бурда.html>бурда́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">burdá</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бурда.html>бурды́</a></b>, <i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> dishwater, slops
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:чай.html>чай</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>а</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:бурда.html>бурда́</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">éto ne čaj, a <b>burdá</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">this tea tastes like dishwater</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:буревестник.html>буреве́стник</a> (26031)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:буря.html>бу́ря</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">búrja</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">storm</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-e-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вестник.html>ве́стник</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">véstnik</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">messenger</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; compare <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">storm petrel</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:буревестник.html>буреве́стник</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">burevéstnik</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:буревестник.html>буреве́стника</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:буревестник.html>буреве́стники</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:буревестник.html>буреве́стников</a></b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:бурелом.html>бурело́м</a> (19729)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>First attested in 1847. <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:буря.html>бу́ря</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">búrja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-e-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ломать.html>лома́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lomátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, calque of  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Windbruch</i>, whence also <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">ветроло́м</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vetrolóm</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> [Arapova].

</p>

***бурка.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:бурка.html>бу́рка</a> (10602)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бурка.html>бу́рка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">búrka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бурка.html>бу́рки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бурка.html>бу́рки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бурка.html>бу́рок</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>burka (male garment from the Caucasus)</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:буркнуть.html>бу́ркнуть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">búrknutʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">бу́ркать</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бурчать.html>бурча́ть</a></b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:бурун.html>буру́н</a> (21919)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бурун.html>буру́н</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">burún</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бурун.html>буруна́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бурун.html>буруны́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бурун.html>буруно́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>breaker, surf</li>
<li>bow wave</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b>бу<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ру́н</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:неодушевленный.html>неодушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:мужской.html>мужско́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 2-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 1b  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка).

***бурундук.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:бурундук.html>бурунду́к</a> (26082)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>A <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Turkic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Turkic languages">Turkic</a></span> borrowing, to be compared with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tatar_language" class="extiw" title="w:Tatar language">Tatar</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="tt">борындык</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="tt-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">borındıq</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">chipmunk</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> or, less likely, a reshaping of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mari_language" class="extiw" title="w:Mari language">Eastern Mari</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="chm">у́рымдо</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="chm-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">úrymdo</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">chipmunk</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бурундук.html>бурунду́к</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">burundúk</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бурундук.html>бурундука́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бурундук.html>бурундуки́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бурундук.html>бурундуко́в</a></b>)

***бурчавший.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:бурчать.html>бурча́вший</a> (16202)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бурчать.html>бурча́вший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">burčávšij</span>)
</p>

***буря.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:буря.html>бу́ря</a> (4180)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*buřa</i>, akin to Bulgarian <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="bg"><a href = vnd.unilang:буря.html>бу́ря</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="bg-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">burja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, Slovene <i class="Latn mention" lang="sl">burja</i>, Polish <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">burza</i>,  Serbo-Croatian <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="sh"><a href = vnd.unilang:бурый.html>бура</a></i>/<i class="Latn mention" lang="sh">bura</i>, Slovak <i class="Latn mention" lang="sk">búrka</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">tempest</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="sk">búrať</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to crush</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Non-Slavic cognates include Old Norse <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">byrr</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">fair wind</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, Latin <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">furo</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">I rage, rave</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, Sanskrit <i class="Deva mention" lang="sa">भुरति</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="sa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bhurati</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">stir, palpitate</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare also <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Turkish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Turkish language">Turkish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="tr">bora</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">squall</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:буря.html>бу́ря</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">búrja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:буря.html>бу́ри</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:буря.html>бу́ри</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:буря.html>бу́рь</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">meteorology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> storm, tempest
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>В</a> бана́ново-лимо́нном сингапу́ре, <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:буря.html>бу́ре</a></b></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">V banánovo-limónnom Singapúre, v <b>búre</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">In Singapore, rich in bananas and lemons, in <b>the storm</b> (from "<a href = vnd.unilang:магнолия.html>Магно́лия</a>" by <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Alexander_Vertinsky" class="extiw" title="w:Alexander Vertinsky">Alexander Vertinsky</a>)</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

</p>
